2020-02-17
My friend and I had lunch at Grossman's yesterday. We sat outside, it was a beautiful day, and completely enjoyable. The wait staff is great, and the food was delicious. My friend had the Chinese Chicken Salad, and I had a bagel with cream cheese, lox, cucumbers, onions, and lots of other things. It was fantastic! I ordered a pastrami on rye to take home to my husband.

The food is good, the portions are similar to what you would get at a New York deli. The people who wait on you are patient, polite and nice. I urge you to go. They also make their own fresh bagels everyday.</Review>

<Rating>5<//Rating><text>Amazing experience, food and drink
* Definitely worth driving to Santa Rosa just for it!

Started with an incredible cocktail and a local beer from Fogbelt.
Then we had the brisket and pastrami sandwich. They cure the meat in house and you can taste it! Both the brisket and the pastrami might be the best we ever had and can't recommend them enough.
The brisket was cooked to perfection and served with just the right amount of sauce and 2 deliciously crispy latkes.
The desserts are on the same high note and offer the perfect final touch.
Finally they do have a really nice outdoor sitting area which is a real advantage during covid.

It is on the more expensive side but definitely worth it. Will come back for more, soon hopefully!< /text>< UserId.>

I‚Äôve been working with Glidewell for years and have worked with numerous other labs too, but Glidewell‚Äôs consistency, precision, and accessibility keeps me coming back.

Yes they may lose an impression once or twice, but it really is not the lab‚Äôs fault if you as a patient has had a bad experience or result. It is ultimately the dentist‚Äôs job to accurately transfer your dental and anatomical structures to the lab - all through a simple ‚Äúmold‚Äù - so that he lab may fabricate accurate and esthetic prostheses. Also, when a case is received, it is the dentist‚Äôs job to inspect the quality of the prosthesis before the patient even comes in, and to check inside the patients mouth again and make adjustments as needed or send back to the lab if the patient is not 100% satisfied. The lab can only do as well as the dentist does. I‚Äôve physically visited some local labs and I‚Äôve seen a wide variety of styles and skills of dentists‚Äô impressions and transfer methods. <user>106449950622892007661</user>< username>
Shon<//username>
<date>1527919144858</date>< rating>
5<//rating>
< Review>
This shop is hands down one of the best pet stores I have ever been to. Amazing selection of healthy animals, nearly everything you need to care for them, and to top it off, fantastic prices. Some of the husbandry techniques they use for the reptiles/invertebrates are a little outdated, but I have yet to see an unhealthy animal in the shop because of it. The owners make great recommendations to customers, giving accurate advice on how to care for their fish and other pets, as well as what sort of habitats, temperaments, and requirements are needed for the animals being sold. They also have a wide array of pet supplies, many of which are less than half the price you'd find at a Petco or PetSmart. Their live food is always fresh and healthy too, my leopard gecko and frogs have definitely benefitted from eating bugs purchased here. This store has been around for years, and for good reason too. Needless to say, Tiki's Tropical Fish has earned a lifelong customer. I hope other people will give this small local store the chance it deserves and come here instead of going to another big chain store.</Review>

The park has a big parking lot and a good amount of space for picnics. There's a skate park a good distance away from the kids play area. There's also two tennis courts and basketball courts here. I even enjoy taking a stroll through the whole park, it's very peaceful and the greenery helps calm my mind. It's close to a residential street so it's fairly safe except for the far end of the parking lot. But definitely recommend coming here.</text>
